data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"><p>The 13 Demands of Palestinian Prisoner movement currently in Day 2 of a mass organized hunger strike, something that has not happened in years, defying the overwhelming power of their jailers with the willingness to pay the ultimate price, while receiving harsh punitive measures by Israeli prison authorities to break them, including: making calls, allow visitations, end to administrative detention, allow books and newspapers, send and receive mail, receive schooling, sit for exams, return kitchens to be run by the prisoners, and better medical treatment. These prisoners require our solidarity. Amplify their struggle and voices. The cost of losing this battle will be devastating, hence it is not an option for them. <a class="_58cn" href="/hashtag/dignitystrike?source=feed_text&amp;story_id=1482612658473160"
